<p id="info-hasil" style="margin-top:0.5rem;font-size:0.8rem;color:#888;"></p>

<script>
function filterTabel(kata) {
  var rows = document.querySelectorAll("#tbody-tile tr");
  var q = kata.toLowerCase();
  var tampil = 0;
  rows.forEach(function(row) {
    var teks = row.textContent.toLowerCase();
    if (teks.includes(q)) {
      row.style.display = "";
      tampil++;
    } else {
      row.style.display = "none";
    }
  });
  var info = document.getElementById("info-hasil");
  if (kata !== "") {
    info.textContent = "Menampilkan " + tampil + " dari 493 tile";
  } else {
    info.textContent = "";
  }
}
</script>
